The breakfast buffet is on the 37th floor, but there is no view. You can start eating at 6:30 and finish at 9:00 on weekdays and 10:00 on weekends and holidays. The variety of breakfast is not particularly large, but it is filling. There are both Chinese and Western styles. There are more varieties of Chinese hot dishes than expected, and the taste is pretty good. There are noodles, rice noodles, rice cakes, etc. in the open stall, and the waiters will take the initiative to come Collect the plates and say excuse me.
You can park for free at the hotel. There are very few parking spaces on the ground. The underground garage is okay. Follow the signs and park near the hotel elevator hall for easy entry and exit. Every time you go out, you need to go to the front desk to get a parking ticket. When you go out, remember to take the ticket verification exit.
There is a park nearby where you can go for a stroll.
